        <h2 class="text-center h1">your questions, our answers</h2>
        <ul class="faq-group list-unstyled">
                <li class="faq-item">
                  <h3 class="faq-content-title headline-primary">WHAT CAN A WEBSITE DO FOR MY BUSINESS?</h3>
                  <div style="overflow: hidden; display: none;" class="faq-content">
                    <p>Most people looking for goods or services start on the web. Unfortunately, many small businesses can't afford to pay someone else to build their website. That's where GoDaddy comes in  we can show you <strong>how to create a website</strong> for yourself.</p>
<p>Design your own <strong>website</strong> fast to ensure your customers find you early  while they're still shopping around. In this fast-changing Internet age, there's no time like the present.</p>
<p>Don't have a business? You'll want a website to connect with family, friends and others who share your passions. Luckily, it's easy and inexpensive to <strong>make your own website</strong>.</p>
<p>For more information, see <a href="https://www.godaddy.com/websites/website-builder/how-to-build-a-website">How Do I Build a Website</a>?</p>

                  </div>
                </li>
                <li class="faq-item">
                  <h3 class="faq-content-title headline-primary">CAN I LEARN HOW TO MAKE A WEBSITE?</h3>
                  <div style="overflow: hidden; display: none;" class="faq-content">
                    <p>Yes! If you'd like to create a website but have limited technical skills, don't worry. GoDaddy's easy, do-it-yourself Website Builder is just what you need.</p>
<p>You have the ideas. We have the tools to make them a reality.</p>
<p>Just scroll through our library of <strong>website templates</strong>, choose a layout you like, adjust the colors, replace the photos with your own or any of the 8,700 included stock photos and add your own text. With GoDaddy Website Builder<sup></sup>, building your own website is actually fun.</p>
<p>Want to see how easy it is to get a website online? Check out <a href="https://www.godaddy.com/websites/website-builder/how-to-publish-a-website">How to Publish a Website</a>.</p>

                  </div>
                </li>
                <li class="faq-item">
                  <h3 class="faq-content-title headline-primary">WHAT SHOULD I LOOK FOR IN A WEB BUILDER?</h3>
                  <div style="overflow: hidden; display: none;" class="faq-content">
                    <p>Be sure to look for a variety of <strong>website templates</strong> and a nice big library of free photos. Also, a good website builder has the flexibility to let you make changes on the fly when your next brilliant idea strikes.</p>
<p>You'll also want to check to be sure you can switch to a new website template without losing the text you've already added. Short on time? Look for <strong>pre-built</strong> websites with words and pictures already filled in.</p>
<p>Although technology has come a long way, many people still need help as they learn <strong>how to create a website</strong>. Luckily, GoDaddy is here with answers.</p>
<p>Call our customer service any time day or night with general questions on <strong>how to make a website</strong> or specific help with creating a slideshow, for example, or adding a Facebook<sup></sup> feed to your website.</p>
<p>For more information, see <a href="https://www.godaddy.com/websites/website-builder/website-template">What are Website Templates</a>?</p>

                  </div>
                </li>
                <li class="faq-item">
                  <h3 class="faq-content-title headline-primary">HOW CAN I USE MY WEBSITE?</h3>
                  <div style="overflow: hidden; display: none;" class="faq-content">
                    <p>Once you become familiar with your website builder from GoDaddy and <strong>learn how to make a Website</strong>, the possibilities are endless. Are you a doctor or lawyer, or are you still searching for the perfect job? You can create a <strong>Doctor Website</strong> or a <strong>Legal Website</strong> to attract new local clients. If you're a job searcher, you can easily make a <strong>Resume Website</strong> to show off skills, experiences and references that will help you land that dream job.</p>
<p>Post and <strong>share pictures</strong> of the kids. <strong>Promote your business</strong> product line. Websites are so versatile, everyone should have one.</p>

                  </div>
                </li>
                <li class="faq-item">
                  <h3 class="faq-content-title headline-primary">HOW ABOUT A SHOPPING CART?</h3>
                  <div style="overflow: hidden; display: none;" class="faq-content">
                    <p>Want to sell products or services online? Add a <a href="https://www.godaddy.com/websites/online-store">shopping cart</a>. Eager to attract more visitors to your website? Optimize your website for search engines. You can find free articles on everything from how to create a website to using social media to promote your business at <a href="https://support.godaddy.com">Support.GoDaddy.com</a>.</p>
<p>For more information, see <a href="https://www.godaddy.com/websites/website-builder/build-a-website">Tips to Build a Website</a>.</p>

                  </div>
                </li>

<script>
  (function() {
    function check(exp, cmp, version) {
      if (!exp || !exp.exec) { return; }
      var match = exp.exec(navigator.userAgent);
      var found = false;
  
      if (match && match.length > 1) {
        var major = parseInt(match[1], 10);
        found = cmp.indexOf('=') > -1 && major === version ? true :
          cmp.indexOf('<') === 0 && major < version ? true :
          cmp.indexOf('>') === 0 && major > version ? true :
          false;
      }
  
      if (!found) { return; }
  
      window.location = '//img1.wsimg.com/ux/1.3.21-brand/html/browser-upgrade.en.html' +
        '?shopper=' + uxel.data.shopperId +
        '&pl=' + uxel.data.plId;
    }
  
    if (ux.config['disableBrowserDeprecation'] === true) { return; }
  
    var blocks = [{"ua":"ie","major":7,"compare":"<=","exp":{}}];
  
    if (blocks && blocks.length > 0) {
      for (var cfg in blocks) {
        check(cfg.exp, cfg.compare, cfg.major);
      }
    }
  
    ux.ready(function() {
      $('<div id="uxh-browser-dep" />')
        .prependTo(document.body)
        .sfBrowser({"ignored":[{"ua":"mobile","exp":{}}],"block":[{"ua":"ie","major":7,"compare":"<=","exp":{}}],"warn":[{"ua":"ie","major":8,"compare":"<=","strict":true,"exp":{}}]});
    });
  
  })();
</script>

<script>
  (function() {
    function addOnLoad(func) {
      window.onload = (function(old) {
        return (typeof(old) === 'function') ? function() { old(); func(); } : func;
      })(window.onload);
    }
    addOnLoad(function() {
      var parent = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
      var el = document.createElement('script');
      el.src = '//img1.wsimg.com/ux/1.3.21-brand/js/uxcore.en.min.js';
      parent.appendChild(el);
      ux.ready(function() {
        ux.jQuery = $;
        var el2 = document.createElement('script');
        el2.src = '//img1.wsimg.com/ux/eldorado/1.5.19/js/salesheader.min.js';
        parent.appendChild(el2);
      });
    });
  })();
</script><!-- Manifest salesheader -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
(function() {
  function asyncLoad(src, callback) {
    if(window.addEventListener) {
      window.addEventListener('load', function () { insertScript(src, callback); } ,false);
    }
    else if(window.attachEvent) {
      window.attachEvent('onload', function () { insertScript(src, callback); } );
    }
    else {
      setTimeout(function() { insertScript(src, callback); }, 2000);
    }
  }

  function insertScript(src, callback) {
    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.type = 'text/javascript';
    script.src = src;

    if (callback) {
      script.onload = callback;
    }

    document.body.appendChild(script);
  }

  window.lazy = window.lazy || {};
  window.lazy.asyncLoad = asyncLoad;
})();
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    lazy.asyncLoad('https://img1.wsimg.com/cms/sales/js/sales-cms-20150526.min.js');
  </script>
